<h1 class="firstHeading mw-first-heading" id="firstHeading"><span class="mw-page-title-main">函数</span></h1>
<div class="vector-body" id="bodyContent">
<div class="noprint" id="siteSub">维基百科，自由的百科全书</div>
<div id="contentSub"></div>
<div id="contentSub2"></div>
<div id="jump-to-nav"></div>
<a class="mw-jump-link" href="#mw-head">跳到导航</a>
<a class="mw-jump-link" href="#searchInput">跳到搜索</a>
<div class="mw-body-content mw-content-ltr" dir="ltr" id="mw-content-text" lang="zh"><div class="mw-parser-output"><div class="noteTA" id="noteTA-92f7f62c"><div class="noteTA-group"><div data-noteta-group="Math" data-noteta-group-source="module"></div></div><div class="noteTA-local"><div data-noteta-code="zh-cn:程序; zh-tw:程式;"></div></div></div><div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note"><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:%E6%B6%88%E6%AD%A7%E4%B9%89" title="Wikipedia:消歧义"><img alt="Disambig gray.svg" data-file-height="168" data-file-width="220" decoding="async" height="19" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5f/Disambig_gray.svg/25px-Disambig_gray.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5f/Disambig_gray.svg/38px-Disambig_gray.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5f/Disambig_gray.svg/50px-Disambig_gray.svg.png 2x" width="25"/></a>  此条目介绍的是数学中的函数。关于程序设计中的函数，请见「<b><a href="/wiki/%E5%AD%90%E7%A8%8B%E5%BA%8F" title="子程序">子程序</a></b>」。</div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Function_machine2.svg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="189" data-file-width="191" decoding="async" height="218" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3b/Function_machine2.svg/220px-Function_machine2.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3b/Function_machine2.svg/330px-Function_machine2.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3b/Function_machine2.svg/440px-Function_machine2.svg.png 2x" width="220"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Function_machine2.svg" title="放大"></a></div>函数<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle f}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>f</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle f}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="f" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/132e57acb643253e7810ee9702d9581f159a1c61" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:1.279ex; height:2.509ex;"/></span> 就像机器或<a href="/wiki/%E9%BB%91%E7%AE%B1" title="黑箱">黑箱</a>，给予输入值<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle x}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>x</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle x}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="x" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/87f9e315fd7e2ba406057a97300593c4802b53e4" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.33ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>便产生唯一输出值<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle f(x)}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>f</mi>
<mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
<mi>x</mi>
<mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle f(x)}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="f(x)" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/202945cce41ecebb6f643f31d119c514bec7a074" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:4.418ex; height:2.843ex;"/></span></div></div></div>
<p><b>函数</b>（英语：<span lang="en">Function</span>）是<a href="/wiki/%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6" title="数学">数学</a>描述对应关系的一种特殊<a href="/wiki/%E9%9B%86%E5%90%88_(%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6)" title="集合 (数学)">集合</a>。
</p>

<h2><span id=".E7.B0.A1.E4.BB.8B"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="简介">简介</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%87%BD%E6%95%B0&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="编辑章节：简介">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>若<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle x}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>x</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle x}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="x" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/87f9e315fd7e2ba406057a97300593c4802b53e4" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.33ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>是<a href="/wiki/%E5%AE%9E%E6%95%B0" title="实数">实数</a>，以<a href="/wiki/%E6%9C%89%E5%BA%8F%E5%AF%B9" title="有序对">有序对</a> <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle (x,\,x^{2})}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
<mi>x</mi>
<mo>,</mo>
<mspace width="thinmathspace"></mspace>
<msup>
<mi>x</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mn>2</mn>
</mrow>
</msup>
<mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle (x,\,x^{2})}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle (x,\,x^{2})}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/ad7ded32455e2243589efa3cf4362edb44f0f94d" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:6.944ex; height:3.176ex;"/></span> 为元素所构成的集合就是一个函数。直观上代表＂输入＂ <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle x}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>x</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle x}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="x" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/87f9e315fd7e2ba406057a97300593c4802b53e4" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.33ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span> 就可以得到唯一值 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle x^{2}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<msup>
<mi>x</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mn>2</mn>
</mrow>
</msup>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle x^{2}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="x^{2}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/cf0bf28fd28f45d07e1ceb909ce333c18c558c93" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:2.384ex; height:2.676ex;"/></span> 的对应关系。
</p><p>一般会以英文字母 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle f,\,g,\,h}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>f</mi>
<mo>,</mo>
<mspace width="thinmathspace"></mspace>
<mi>g</mi>
<mo>,</mo>
<mspace width="thinmathspace"></mspace>
<mi>h</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle f,\,g,\,h}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle f,\,g,\,h}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/e1b1973006bcbcc0d3d1a2a302e640c5bb5e184d" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:6.576ex; height:2.509ex;"/></span>  表示函数，并把 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle x}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>x</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle x}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="x" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/87f9e315fd7e2ba406057a97300593c4802b53e4" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.33ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span> 依据函数 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle f}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>f</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle f}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="f" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/132e57acb643253e7810ee9702d9581f159a1c61" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:1.279ex; height:2.509ex;"/></span> 的对应规则所得到的值写作<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle f(x)}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>f</mi>
<mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
<mi>x</mi>
<mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle f(x)}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="f(x)" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/202945cce41ecebb6f643f31d119c514bec7a074" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:4.418ex; height:2.843ex;"/></span> ，并读作"<i>f of x"</i>。函数的概念不限于数之间的对应关系，例定义函数 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \operatorname {Capital} }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>Capital</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \operatorname {Capital} }</annotation>
</semantics>

</p><p>直观上的"多变数函数"其实也可以概括到一般函数的定义里。例如算式 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle x\times y}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</p><p>数学中，<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%B0%8D%E6%87%89" title="对应">对应</a>、<a href="/wiki/%E6%98%A0%E5%B0%84" title="映射">映射</a>、<a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%8F%98%E6%8D%A2&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="变换（页面不存在）">变换</a>通常都是函数的别称，但也可能有别的意思，如在<a href="/wiki/%E6%8B%93%E6%89%91%E5%AD%A6" title="拓扑学">拓扑学</a>的映射有时代表的是<a href="/wiki/%E8%BF%9E%E7%BB%AD%E5%87%BD%E6%95%B0" title="连续函数">连续函数</a>。
</p><p>在<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E9%A1%9E%E5%9E%8B%E8%AB%96" title="类型论">类型论</a>的<a href="/wiki/%CE%9B%E6%BC%94%E7%AE%97" title="Λ演算">λ演算</a>中，"对应关系"可以是作为一个原始概念(也就是无定义名词)，而不像上述的定义把函数视为<a href="/wiki/%E9%9B%86%E5%90%88_(%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6)" title="集合 (数学)">集合</a>的衍伸物。
</p>
<h2><span id=".E5.8E.86.E5.8F.B2"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="历史">历史</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%87%BD%E6%95%B0&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="编辑章节：历史">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>函数这个数学名词是<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%8E%B1%E5%B8%83%E5%B0%BC%E5%85%B9" title="莱布尼兹">莱布尼兹</a>在1694年开始使用的，用来描述跟<a href="/wiki/%E6%9B%B2%E7%BA%BF" title="曲线">曲线</a>相关的一个量，如曲线的<a href="/wiki/%E6%96%9C%E7%8E%87" title="斜率">斜率</a>或者曲线上的某一点。莱布尼兹所指的函数现在被称作<a href="/wiki/%E5%AF%BC%E6%95%B0" title="导数">可导函数</a>，数学家之外的普通人一般接触到的函数即属此类。对于可导函数可以讨论它的<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%87%BD%E6%95%B0%E6%9E%81%E9%99%90" title="函数极限">极限</a>和<a href="/wiki/%E5%AF%BC%E6%95%B0" title="导数">导数</a>，此两者描述了函数输出值的变化同输入值变化的关系，是<a href="/wiki/%E5%BE%AE%E7%A7%AF%E5%88%86%E5%AD%A6" title="微积分学">微积分学</a>的基础。中文的“<b>函数</b>”一词由<a href="/wiki/%E6%B8%85%E6%9C%9D" title="清朝">清朝</a>数学家<a href="/wiki/%E6%9D%8E%E5%96%84%E5%85%B0" title="李善兰">李善兰</a>译出。其《代数学》书中解释：“凡此变数中函（包含）彼变数者，则此为彼之函数”。
</p>
<ul><li>1718年，<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%BA%A6%E7%BF%B0%C2%B7%E4%BC%AF%E5%8A%AA%E5%88%A9" title="约翰·伯努利">约翰·伯努利</a>把函数定义为“一个变量的函数是指由这个变量和常量以任何一种方式组成的一种量。”</li>
<li>1748年，伯努利的学生<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%AC%A7%E6%8B%89" title="欧拉">欧拉</a>在《无穷分析引论》一书中说：“一个<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%8F%98%E9%87%8F" title="变量">变量</a>的函数是由该变量和一些数或<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%B8%B8%E9%87%8F" title="常量">常量</a>以任何一种方式构成的<a href="/wiki/%E8%A7%A3%E6%9E%90%E8%A7%A3" title="解析解">解析表达式</a>”，例如<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle f(x)=\sin(x)+x^{2}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>f</mi>
<mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
<mi>x</mi>
<mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
<mo>=</mo>
<mi>sin</mi>
<mo>⁡<!-- ⁡ --></mo>
<mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
<mi>x</mi>
<mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
<mo>+</mo>
<msup>
<mi>x</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mn>2</mn>
</mrow>
</msup>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle f(x)=\sin(x)+x^{2}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle f(x)=\sin(x)+x^{2}}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/b0cba2465cb3b055c703945cd06b33c71190aa15" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:18.735ex; height:3.176ex;"/></span>。</li>
<li>1775年，欧拉在《微分学原理》一书中又提出了函数的一个定义：“如果某些量以如下方式依赖于另一些量，即当后者变化时，前者本身也发生变化，则称前一些量是后一些量的函数。”</li>
<li>19世纪的数学家开始对数学的各个分支进行形式化。<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%BB%B4%E5%B0%94%E6%96%AF%E7%89%B9%E6%8B%89%E6%96%AF" title="维尔斯特拉斯">维尔斯特拉斯</a>倡议将微积分学建立在<a href="/wiki/%E7%AE%97%E6%9C%AF" title="算术">算术</a>，而不是<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%87%A0%E4%BD%95" title="几何">几何</a>的基础上，这种主张较趋向于欧拉的定义。</li>
<li>函数的定义得以扩展之后，数学家便能对一些“奇怪”的数学对象进行研究，例如处处不可导的连续函数。这些函数曾经被认为只具有理论价值，迟至20世纪初时它们仍被视作“怪物”。稍后，人们发现这些函数在对如<a href="/wiki/%E5%B8%83%E6%9C%97%E8%BF%90%E5%8A%A8" title="布朗运动">布朗运动</a>之类的物理现象进行建模时有重要的作用。</li>
<li>到19世纪末，数学家开始尝试利用<a href="/wiki/%E9%9B%86%E5%90%88%E8%AE%BA" title="集合论">集合论</a>来进行数学的形式化。他们试图将每一个数学对象都定义为<a href="/wiki/%E9%9B%86%E5%90%88_(%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6)" title="集合 (数学)">集合</a>。<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%8B%84%E5%88%A9%E5%85%8B%E9%9B%B7" title="狄利克雷">狄利克雷</a>给出了现代正式的函数定义（参见下文<a href="#正式定义">#正式定义</a>）。在他的定义下，函数被视作<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6%E5%85%B3%E7%B3%BB" title="数学关系">数学关系</a>的特例。然而对于实际应用的情况，现代定义和欧拉定义的区别可以忽略不计。</li></ul>
<h2><span id=".E6.AD.A3.E5.BC.8F.E5.AE.9A.E7.BE.A9"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="正式定义">正式定义</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%87%BD%E6%95%B0&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="编辑章节：正式定义">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:227px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Cubicpoly.svg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1000" data-file-width="1000" decoding="async" height="225" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/33/Cubicpoly.svg/225px-Cubicpoly.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/33/Cubicpoly.svg/338px-Cubicpoly.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/33/Cubicpoly.svg/450px-Cubicpoly.svg.png 2x" width="225"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Cubicpoly.svg" title="放大"></a></div>函数<i>f</i>的部分图像。每个实数的<i>x</i>都与<i>f</i>（<i>x</i>） = <i>x</i><sup>3</sup> − 9<i>x</i>相联系。</div></div></div>
<p>函数( <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle f}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>f</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle f}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="f" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/132e57acb643253e7810ee9702d9581f159a1c61" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:1.279ex; height:2.509ex;"/></span> )是一种特殊的<a href="/wiki/%E4%BA%8C%E5%85%83%E5%85%B3%E7%B3%BB" title="二元关系">二元关系</a> (也就是元素都是 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle (x,\,y)}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
<mi>x</mi>
<mo>,</mo>
<mspace width="thinmathspace"></mspace>
<mi>y</mi>
<mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle (x,\,y)}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle (x,\,y)}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/0e7afe5870de593e694568d1c4b0b95c6ac50777" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:5.716ex; height:2.843ex;"/></span> 这样形式的二元<a href="/wiki/%E6%9C%89%E5%BA%8F%E5%AF%B9" title="有序对">有序对</a>的集合) ，满足
</p>
<ul><li>对任意 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle x,\,y,\,y^{\prime }}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>x</mi>
<mo>,</mo>
<mspace width="thinmathspace"></mspace>
<mi>y</mi>
<mo>,</mo>
<mspace width="thinmathspace"></mspace>
<msup>
<mi>y</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi class="MJX-variant" mathvariant="normal">′<!-- ′ --></mi>
</mrow>
</msup>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle x,\,y,\,y^{\prime }}</annotation>
</semantics>

<p>若以正式的逻辑符号表述就是(设下面这条<a href="/wiki/%E5%90%88%E5%BC%8F%E5%85%AC%E5%BC%8F" title="合式公式">合式公式</a>简记为 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle {\mathcal {A}}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</p>

<p>也就是直观上，可以把有序对 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle (x,\,y)}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle (x,\,y)}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/0e7afe5870de593e694568d1c4b0b95c6ac50777" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:5.716ex; height:2.843ex;"/></span> 看成 (<i>输入值</i>, <i>输出值</i>)；而函数本身是穷举输出入值来详尽定义的对应规则。而且依照函数 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle f}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<semantics>

<semantics>

</semantics>

</p>
<h3><span id=".E5.87.BD.E6.95.B8.E5.80.BC.E7.9A.84.E7.B0.A1.E8.A8.98"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="函数值的简记">函数值的简记</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%87%BD%E6%95%B0&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="编辑章节：函数值的简记">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>习惯上把 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle (x,\,y)\in f}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
<mi>x</mi>
<mo>,</mo>
<mspace width="thinmathspace"></mspace>
<mi>y</mi>
<mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
<mo>∈<!-- ∈ --></mo>
<mi>f</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle (x,\,y)\in f}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle (x,\,y)\in f}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/42699a7734684ad5072a7f21ce4f6d3bac02a02b" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:9.835ex; height:2.843ex;"/></span> 等价的写为 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle y=f(x)}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>y</mi>
<mo>=</mo>

<mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
</mstyle>

<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle y=f(x)}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="y=f(x)" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/2311a6a75c54b0ea085a381ba472c31d59321514" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:8.672ex; height:2.843ex;"/></span> 。但事实上， <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle f(x)}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle f(x)}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="f(x)" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/202945cce41ecebb6f643f31d119c514bec7a074" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:4.418ex; height:2.843ex;"/></span> 是在<a href="/wiki/%E4%B8%80%E9%98%B6%E9%80%BB%E8%BE%91" title="一阶逻辑">一阶逻辑</a><a href="/wiki/%E5%85%AC%E7%90%86%E5%8C%96%E9%9B%86%E5%90%88%E8%AE%BA" title="公理化集合论">公理化集合论</a>下，基于 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle {\mathcal {A}}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi class="MJX-tex-caligraphic" mathvariant="script">A</mi>
</mrow>
</mrow>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle {\mathcal {A}}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\mathcal {A}}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/280ae03440942ab348c2ca9b8db6b56ffa9618f8" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.903ex; height:2.343ex;"/></span> 所确保的唯一性，而新增的双元<a href="/wiki/%E4%B8%80%E9%98%B6%E9%80%BB%E8%BE%91#函数符号" title="一阶逻辑">函数符号</a> ( <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle x}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>x</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle x}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="x" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/87f9e315fd7e2ba406057a97300593c4802b53e4" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.33ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span> 和 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle f}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>f</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle f}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="f" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/132e57acb643253e7810ee9702d9581f159a1c61" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:1.279ex; height:2.509ex;"/></span> 各为一个变数) ，而它的＂定义＂本质上是以下额外增加的公理 ( 唯一性保证新增这条公理后，"新理论"所拥有的<a href="/wiki/%E4%B8%80%E9%98%B6%E9%80%BB%E8%BE%91#定理与证明" title="一阶逻辑">定理</a>和"旧理论"是一样的，详请参见<a href="/wiki/%E4%B8%80%E9%98%B6%E9%80%BB%E8%BE%91#函数符号与唯一性" title="一阶逻辑">函数符号与唯一性</a>)
</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle [\,\neg ({\mathcal {A}}\wedge {\mathcal {B}})\Rightarrow (f(x)=\varnothing )\,]\vee \{\,({\mathcal {A}}\wedge {\mathcal {B}})\Rightarrow (\forall y)\{\,[\,(x,\,y)\in f\,]\Leftrightarrow [\,y=f(x)\,]\,\}\,\}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mo stretchy="false">[</mo>
<mspace width="thinmathspace"></mspace>
<mi mathvariant="normal">¬<!-- ¬ --></mi>
<mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi class="MJX-tex-caligraphic" mathvariant="script">A</mi>
</mrow>
</mrow>
<mo>∧<!-- ∧ --></mo>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi class="MJX-tex-caligraphic" mathvariant="script">B</mi>
</mrow>
</mrow>
<mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
<mo stretchy="false">⇒<!-- ⇒ --></mo>
<mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
<mi>f</mi>
<mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
<mi>x</mi>
<mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
<mo>=</mo>
<mi class="MJX-variant">∅<!-- ∅ --></mi>
<mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
<mspace width="thinmathspace"></mspace>
<mo stretchy="false">]</mo>
<mo>∨<!-- ∨ --></mo>
<mo fence="false" stretchy="false">{</mo>
<mspace width="thinmathspace"></mspace>
<mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">

<h3><span id=".E5.AE.9A.E7.BE.A9.E5.9F.9F.E8.88.87.E5.80.BC.E5.9F.9F"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="定义域与值域">定义域与值域</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%87%BD%E6%95%B0&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="编辑章节：定义域与值域">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>实用上如果能指出函数 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle f}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle f}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="f" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/132e57acb643253e7810ee9702d9581f159a1c61" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:1.279ex; height:2.509ex;"/></span> 的 "输入值范围" 跟 "输出值范围" ，对数学的讨论是相当方便的；事实上<a href="/wiki/%E5%85%AC%E7%90%86%E5%8C%96%E9%9B%86%E5%90%88%E8%AE%BA" title="公理化集合论">公理化集合论</a>确保对任意集合 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle A}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<p>简单来说， <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle D_{A}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle A}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="A" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/7daff47fa58cdfd29dc333def748ff5fa4c923e3" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.743ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span> 里所有<b>有序对</b>的第一个元素所构成的集合；  <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle I_{A}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<msub>
<mi>I</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi>A</mi>
</mrow>
</msub>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle I_{A}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="I_A" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/fad11afeef762471a89c8a258282a40af27d6516" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:2.488ex; height:2.509ex;"/></span> 是所有搜集所有 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle A}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>A</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle A}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="A" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/7daff47fa58cdfd29dc333def748ff5fa4c923e3" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.743ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span> 里所有<b>有序对</b>的第二个元素所构成的集合，集合论保证了两者一定<b>唯一存在</b>（就算是空集合）。如果 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle A}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>A</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle A}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="A" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/7daff47fa58cdfd29dc333def748ff5fa4c923e3" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.743ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span> 本身就是函数的话，直观上 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle D_{A}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<msub>
<mi>D</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi>A</mi>
</mrow>
</msub>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle D_{A}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle D_{A}}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/b78af4a9d2d8aaec85ea4e6b0f997a31def04311" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:3.389ex; height:2.509ex;"/></span> 就是＂输入值范围＂，所以被称为<a href="/wiki/%E5%AE%9A%E4%B9%89%E5%9F%9F" title="定义域">定义域</a>；而直观上  <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle I_{A}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<msub>
<mi>I</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi>A</mi>
</mrow>
</msub>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle I_{A}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="I_A" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/fad11afeef762471a89c8a258282a40af27d6516" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:2.488ex; height:2.509ex;"/></span> 就是 ＂输出值范围＂，所以被称为<a href="/wiki/%E5%80%BC%E5%9F%9F" title="值域">值域</a>。
</p><p>所以在 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle f}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="f" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/132e57acb643253e7810ee9702d9581f159a1c61" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:1.279ex; height:2.509ex;"/></span> 是函数的情况下，有以下惯用的记号
</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle f:X\to Y}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<mi>X</mi>
<mo stretchy="false">→<!-- → --></mo>
<mi>Y</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle f:X\to Y}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="f:X\to Y" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/abd1e080abef4bbdab67b43819c6431e7561361c" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:10.583ex; height:2.509ex;"/></span></dd></dl>
<p>这个记号严格上来说代表
</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle (D_{f}=X)\wedge (I_{f}\subseteq Y)}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
<msub>
<mi>I</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi>f</mi>
</mrow>
</msub>
<mo>⊆<!-- ⊆ --></mo>
<mi>Y</mi>
<mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle (D_{f}=X)\wedge (I_{f}\subseteq Y)}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle (D_{f}=X)\wedge (I_{f}\subseteq Y)}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/59b8e95ce7c822dc8549f7af39b48c07d56f3af8" style="vertical-align: -1.005ex; width:21.371ex; height:3.009ex;"/></span></dd></dl>
<p>也就是函数 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle f}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="f" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/132e57acb643253e7810ee9702d9581f159a1c61" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:1.279ex; height:2.509ex;"/></span> 的＂输入值范围＂为 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle X}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>

<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>X</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle X}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="X" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/68baa052181f707c662844a465bfeeb135e82bab" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.98ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span> ， ＂输出值范围＂包含于 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle Y}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>

</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="Y" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/961d67d6b454b4df2301ac571808a3538b3a6d3f" style="vertical-align: -0.171ex; width:1.773ex; height:2.009ex;"/></span>。 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle Y}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</semantics>

</p><p>属于定义域 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle D_{f}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>

<mi>f</mi>
</mrow>
</msub>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle D_{f}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle D_{f}}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/13b8420d715315c8e8b57f178a1b3a8512bd0959" style="vertical-align: -1.005ex; width:3.061ex; height:2.843ex;"/></span> 的元素 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle x}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<mi>x</mi>
<mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle f(x)}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="f(x)" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/202945cce41ecebb6f643f31d119c514bec7a074" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:4.418ex; height:2.843ex;"/></span> 则被俗称为<b>因变量（</b>dependent variable），但是这跟实验上的<a href="/wiki/%E8%87%AA%E5%8F%98%E9%87%8F%E5%92%8C%E5%9B%A0%E5%8F%98%E9%87%8F" title="自变量和因变量">自变量和因变量</a>是稍有不同的，因为一个是以现实手段操纵所得到的实验值之间的关联，但另一个是源于集合论的抽象逻辑概念。
</p>
<h3><span id=".E4.B8.80.E5.B0.8D.E4.B8.80.E8.88.87.E6.BB.BF.E5.B0.84"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="一对一与满射">一对一与满射</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%87%BD%E6%95%B0&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="编辑章节：一对一与满射">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>满足
</p>
<ul><li>对任意 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle y,\,x,\,x^{\prime }}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<p>的函数 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle f}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle f^{-1}:=\{\,p\,|\,(\exists x)(\exists y)[\,p=(y,\,x)\,\wedge \,y=f(x)\,]\,\}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle f^{-1}:=\{\,p\,|\,(\exists x)(\exists y)[\,p=(y,\,x)\,\wedge \,y=f(x)\,]\,\}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle f^{-1}:=\{\,p\,|\,(\exists x)(\exists y)[\,p=(y,\,x)\,\wedge \,y=f(x)\,]\,\}}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/c98c482cef684eca46e2d6e58f4428914c1270c0" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:45.857ex; height:3.176ex;"/></span></dd></dl><p>
也是一个函数，称为 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle f}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>f</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle f}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="f" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/132e57acb643253e7810ee9702d9581f159a1c61" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:1.279ex; height:2.509ex;"/></span> 的<a href="/wiki/%E5%8F%8D%E5%87%BD%E6%95%B8" title="反函数">反函数</a>。</p><div class="center"><div class="thumb tnone"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:344px"><div class="thumbimage noresize" style="width:342px;">
<div style="background-color: #F9F9F9; padding-left: 5px; margin: 0;">

</div></div></div><div class="thumbcaption"><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle y=x^{2}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<style data-mw-deduplicate="TemplateStyles:r70089473/mw-parser-output/.tmulti">.mw-parser-output .tmulti .thumbinner{display:flex;flex-direction:column}.mw-parser-output .tmulti .thumbcaption{text-align:left}.mw-parser-output .tmulti .trow>.thumbcaption{text-align:center}}</style></p><div class="thumb tmulti tnone center"><div class="thumbinner" class="thumbcaption">（2）一对一但非完全对应。<i>X</i>的元素1未与<i>Y</i>的任一元素相关。因此这是<b>偏函数</b>，而<i>不是</i>函数。</div></div><div class="tsingle" style="width:252px;max-width:252px"><div class="thumbimage"><a <h2><span id=".E5.87.BD.E6.95.B0.E5.9B.BE.E5.BD.A2"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="函数图形">函数图形</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%87%BD%E6%95%B0&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="编辑章节：函数图形">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:344px"><div class="thumbimage noresize" style="width:342px;">
<div style="background-color: #F9F9F9; padding-left: 5px; margin: 0;">
<div style="font-size: 0.8em; text-align: left;">
<link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r65530652" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/><div class="mw-graph mw-graph-always mw-graph-nofallback" data-graph-id="c7efff851348944194c2552a2b9a8cfa707ceb0d" style="min-width:200px;min-height:100px"></div>
</div></div></div><div class="thumbcaption">sin(x)等函数的图形</div></div></div>
<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">主条目：<a href="/wiki/%E5%87%BD%E6%95%B0%E5%9B%BE%E5%BD%A2" title="函数图形">函数图形</a></div>
<p>如果函数 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle f}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>f</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle f}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="f" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/132e57acb643253e7810ee9702d9581f159a1c61" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:1.279ex; height:2.509ex;"/></span> 的值域跟定义域都是实数集合(俗称 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle f}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>f</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle f}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="f" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/132e57acb643253e7810ee9702d9581f159a1c61" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:1.279ex; height:2.509ex;"/></span> 为<b>实函数</b>)，可以x轴代表定义域的范围；y轴代表值域的范围，把函数的每个元素标示在平面<a href="/wiki/%E7%AC%9B%E5%8D%A1%E5%B0%94%E5%9D%90%E6%A0%87%E7%B3%BB" title="笛卡尔坐标系">直角坐标</a>上，这被称为实函数 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle f}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>f</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle f}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="f" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/132e57acb643253e7810ee9702d9581f159a1c61" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:1.279ex; height:2.509ex;"/></span> 在平面上的<b>函数图形</b>。
</p><p>对于"双变数"的实函数 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle g}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">

</mstyle>

</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="g" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/d3556280e66fe2c0d0140df20935a6f057381d77" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:1.116ex; height:2.009ex;"/></span> ，也就是以 (<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle x,\,y,\,z\in \mathbb {R} }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>

<mi mathvariant="double-struck">R</mi>

</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle ((x,\,y),\,z)}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<p>为元素的函数，可以取
</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle D_{x}=\{\,x\,|\,(\exists y)(\exists z)[\,g(x,\,y)=z\,]\,\}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<mi>x</mi>

</msub>
<mo>=</mo>
<mo fence="false" stretchy="false">{</mo>
<mspace width="thinmathspace"></mspace>
<mi>x</mi>
<mspace width="thinmathspace"></mspace>

</mrow>

<mi mathvariant="normal">∃<!-- ∃ --></mi>

<mi>z</mi>

<mspace width="thinmathspace"></mspace>
<mi>g</mi>
<mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
<mi>x</mi>
<mo>,</mo>
<mspace width="thinmathspace"></mspace>
<mi>y</mi>
<mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
<mo>=</mo>
<mi>z</mi>
<mspace width="thinmathspace"></mspace>
<mo stretchy="false">]</mo>
<mspace width="thinmathspace"></mspace>
<mo fence="false" stretchy="false">}</mo>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle D_{x}=\{\,x\,|\,(\exists y)(\exists z)[\,g(x,\,y)=z\,]\,\}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle D_{x}=\{\,x\,|\,(\exists y)(\exists z)[\,g(x,\,y)=z\,]\,\}}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/c9dddbd942ba946433d604d83c67676cfa21bd5c" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:33.578ex; height:2.843ex;"/></span></dd></dl>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle D_{y}=\{\,x\,|\,(\exists x)(\exists z)[\,g(x,\,y)=z\,]\,\}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</semantics>

<p>然后以 x 轴为 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle D_{x}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>

</msub>

</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="D_{x}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/c15427ff95343d483864e9ad5f2f836de676312d" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:3.097ex; height:2.509ex;"/></span> 变化范围；y 轴为 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle D_{y}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>

<mi>y</mi>
</mrow>
</msub>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle D_{y}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle D_{y}}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/7a95004ec6d8f49f4ba24d128be75b682bd85847" style="vertical-align: -1.005ex; width:2.974ex; height:2.843ex;"/></span> 变化范围；最后取z 轴为 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle g}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>g</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle g}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="g" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/d3556280e66fe2c0d0140df20935a6f057381d77" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:1.116ex; height:2.009ex;"/></span> 的<b>函数图形</b>。
</p>
<h3><span id=".E5.AF.A6.E5.87.BD.E6.95.B0.E7.9A.84.E5.88.A4.E5.88.AB"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="实函数的判别">实函数的判别</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%87%BD%E6%95%B0&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="编辑章节：实函数的判别">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>平面上的任意图形可用<b>竖直判别法</b>判断是否为<b>实函数</b>的图形，即图形与任何一条平行于 y 轴的直线不能有一个以上的交点。但实际上这仅仅是函数正式定义的一种应用，因为平行于 y 轴的直线代表的是形如 
</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \{\,p\in {\mathbb {R} }^{2}\,|\,(\exists y\in \mathbb {R} )[\,p=(c,\,y)\,]\,\}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">

<msup>

</mrow>

</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle \{\,p\in {\mathbb {R} }^{2}\,|\,(\exists y\in \mathbb {R} )[\,p=(c,\,y)\,]\,\}}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/e3cab4f2ea350717f6ceecd749e509469bb84ce1" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:31.767ex; height:3.176ex;"/></span></dd></dl>
<p>的集合，也就是此直线交 x 轴于 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle (c,\,0)}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>

<mi>c</mi>
<mo>,</mo>
<mspace width="thinmathspace"></mspace>
<mn>0</mn>

</mstyle>
</mrow>

</semantics>

<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>f</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle f}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="f" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/132e57acb643253e7810ee9702d9581f159a1c61" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:1.279ex; height:2.509ex;"/></span>  的交集就是 
</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \{\,p\in {\mathbb {R} }^{2}\,|\,(\exists y\in \mathbb {R} )[\,p=(c,\,y)\wedge y=f(c)\,]\,\}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<p>而属于这个交集里的平面点<b>最多只能有一个</b>，否则就会跟每个 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle x\in D_{f}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</p>
<h2><span id=".E5.83.8F.E5.92.8C.E5.8E.9F.E5.83.8F"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="像和原像">像和原像</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%87%BD%E6%95%B0&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="编辑章节：像和原像">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p><a href="/wiki/%E5%83%8F_(%E6%95%B8%E5%AD%B8)" title="像 (数学)"><b>像</b></a>可以指两种不同的概念
</p><p>第一种是形如 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle f(x)}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>f</mi>
<mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
<mi>x</mi>
<mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle f(x)}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="f(x)" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/202945cce41ecebb6f643f31d119c514bec7a074" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:4.418ex; height:2.843ex;"/></span> 的<a href="/wiki/%E4%B8%80%E9%98%B6%E9%80%BB%E8%BE%91#项" title="一阶逻辑">项</a>，直观上代表的是依照函数 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle f}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>f</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle f}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="f" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/132e57acb643253e7810ee9702d9581f159a1c61" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:1.279ex; height:2.509ex;"/></span> 的对应规则，使 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle x}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>x</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle x}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="x" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/87f9e315fd7e2ba406057a97300593c4802b53e4" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.33ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span> 能对应到的那个"值"。(严谨的意义请回去参考<a href="/wiki/%E5%87%BD%E6%95%B0#函数值的简记" title="函数">函数值的简记</a>)
</p><p>第二种指的是集合 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle A}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>A</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle A}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="A" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/7daff47fa58cdfd29dc333def748ff5fa4c923e3" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.743ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span> 在函数 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle f}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>f</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle f}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="f" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/132e57acb643253e7810ee9702d9581f159a1c61" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:1.279ex; height:2.509ex;"/></span> 下定义的集合 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle f(A)}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>f</mi>
<mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
<mi>A</mi>
<mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle f(A)}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="f(A)" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/2711c647e5397c7016ee21bbcea53565480bd5e1" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:4.831ex; height:2.843ex;"/></span>
</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle f(A):=\{\,y\,|\,(\exists x\in A)[\,y=f(x)\,]\,\}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>f</mi>
<mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
<mi>A</mi>
<mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
<mo>:=</mo>

<p>沿用同一例子，可以看到 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \{a,b\}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<p>这些特性适合定义域的任意子集<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle A,A_{1}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<h2><span id=".E5.87.BD.E6.95.B8.E7.9A.84.E9.99.90.E5.88.B6.E5.8F.8A.E6.93.B4.E5.BC.B5"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="函数的限制及扩张">函数的限制及扩张</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%87%BD%E6%95%B0&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="编辑章节：函数的限制及扩张">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>若 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle f:X\to Y}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<p>显然为一函数，称为 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle f}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</p><p>反之，若 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle g:X\to Z}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</msub>
<mo>=</mo>
<mi>g</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle f|_{X}=g}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="f|_{X}=g" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/a12705360feaf153cea95f7d9c59c102cc0ad1d9" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:7.772ex; height:2.843ex;"/></span>，那 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle f}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>f</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle f}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="f" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/132e57acb643253e7810ee9702d9581f159a1c61" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:1.279ex; height:2.509ex;"/></span> 称为 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle g}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>g</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle g}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="g" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/d3556280e66fe2c0d0140df20935a6f057381d77" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:1.116ex; height:2.009ex;"/></span> 的<b><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%87%BD%E6%95%B8%E7%9A%84%E6%93%B4%E5%BC%B5&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="函数的扩张（页面不存在）">扩张</a></b>。
</p>
<h2><span id=".E7.82.B9.E6.80.81.E8.BF.90.E7.AE.97"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="点态运算">点态运算</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%87%BD%E6%95%B0&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="编辑章节：点态运算">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>设 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle f:X\to R}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>f</mi>
<mo>:</mo>
<mi>X</mi>
<mo stretchy="false">→<!-- → --></mo>
<mi>R</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle f:X\to R}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle f:X\to R}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/08ed9e02e498dee575b1cdb8f9afedf3b4cd4851" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:10.574ex; height:2.509ex;"/></span> 且 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle g:X\to R}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<mi>R</mi>

</semantics>

<p>也是函数，其中 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle r_{R}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle r_{R}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle r_{R}}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/024f7278656cfcdd8ea5db19a5b2d8ea54355183" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:2.528ex; height:2.009ex;"/></span> 被称为<b>常数函数</b>。
</p>
<h2><span id=".E5.87.BD.E6.95.B0.E7.AF.84.E4.BE.8B"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="函数范例">函数范例</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%87%BD%E6%95%B0&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="编辑章节：函数范例">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">参见：<a href="/wiki/%E5%87%BD%E6%95%B0%E5%88%97%E8%A1%A8" title="函数列表">函数列表</a></div>
<ul><li>首都之于国家（若不把多首都国<a class="external autonumber" href="http://geography.about.com/library/misc/bl2capitals.htm" rel="nofollow">[1]</a> （<a class="external text" href="//web.archive.org/web/20051222162004/http://geography.about.com/library/misc/bl2capitals.htm" rel="nofollow">页面存档备份</a>，存于<a href="/wiki/%E4%BA%92%E8%81%94%E7%BD%91%E6%A1%A3%E6%A1%88%E9%A6%86" title="互联网档案馆">互联网档案馆</a>） 计算在内)。</li>
<li>每个<a href="/wiki/%E8%87%AA%E7%84%B6%E6%95%B0" title="自然数">自然数</a><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle n}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%AF%B9%E6%95%B0%E5%87%BD%E6%95%B0" title="对数函数">对数函数</a>。<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \ln x}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<li>对每个在<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \mathbb {R} ^{2}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<p>常用的数学函数包括<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%A4%9A%E9%A1%B9%E5%BC%8F%E5%87%BD%E6%95%B0" title="多项式函数">多项式函数</a>、<a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E6%A0%B9%E5%BC%8F%E5%87%BD%E6%95%B8&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="根式函数（页面不存在）">根式函数</a>、<a href="/wiki/%E5%B9%82%E5%87%BD%E6%95%B0" title="幂函数">幂函数</a>、<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%AF%B9%E6%95%B0%E5%87%BD%E6%95%B0" title="对数函数">对数函数</a>、<a href="/wiki/%E6%9C%89%E7%90%86%E5%87%BD%E6%95%B8" title="有理函数">有理函数</a>、<a href="/wiki/%E4%B8%89%E8%A7%92%E5%87%BD%E6%95%B0" title="三角函数">三角函数</a>、<a href="/wiki/%E5%8F%8D%E4%B8%89%E8%A7%92%E5%87%BD%E6%95%B0" title="反三角函数">反三角函数</a>等。它们都是<a href="/wiki/%E5%88%9D%E7%AD%89%E5%87%BD%E6%95%B0" title="初等函数">初等函数</a>。非初等函数（或<a href="/wiki/%E7%89%B9%E6%AE%8A%E5%87%BD%E6%95%B0" title="特殊函数">特殊函数</a>）包括<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E4%BC%BD%E9%A9%AC%E5%87%BD%E6%95%B0" title="伽马函数">伽马函数</a>和<a href="/wiki/%E8%B4%9D%E5%A1%9E%E5%B0%94%E5%87%BD%E6%95%B0" title="贝塞尔函数">贝塞尔函数</a>等。
</p>
<h2><span id=".E5.87.BD.E6.95.B8.E7.9A.84.E5.88.86.E9.A1.9E"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="函数的分类">函数的分类</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%87%BD%E6%95%B0&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="编辑章节：函数的分类">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>函数可分为
</p>
<ul><li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%A5%87%E5%87%BD%E6%95%B8" title="奇函数">奇函数</a>或<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%81%B6%E5%87%BD%E6%95%B8" title="偶函数">偶函数</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E9%80%A3%E7%BA%8C%E5%87%BD%E6%95%B8" title="连续函数">连续函数</a>或<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E4%B8%8D%E9%80%A3%E7%BA%8C%E5%87%BD%E6%95%B8" title="不连续函数">不连续函数</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/%E5%AE%9E%E5%87%BD%E6%95%B0" title="实函数">实函数</a>或<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%99%9B%E5%87%BD%E6%95%B8" title="虚函数">虚函数</a></li>
<li><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%B4%94%E9%87%8F%E5%87%BD%E6%95%B8&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="纯量函数（页面不存在）">纯量函数</a>或<a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%90%91%E9%87%8F%E5%87%BD%E6%95%B8&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="向量函数（页面不存在）">向量函数</a></li>
<li><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%8D%95%E8%B0%83%E5%A2%9E%E5%87%BD%E6%95%B0&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="单调增函数（页面不存在）">单调增函数</a>或<a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%8D%95%E8%B0%83%E5%87%8F%E5%87%BD%E6%95%B0&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="单调减函数（页面不存在）">单调减函数</a></li></ul>
<h2><span id=".E8.8C.83.E7.95.B4.E8.AB.96.E8.A7.80.E9.BB.9E.E4.B8.8B.E7.9A.84.E5.87.BD.E6.95.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="范畴论观点下的函数">范畴论观点下的函数</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%87%BD%E6%95%B0&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="编辑章节：范畴论观点下的函数">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">参见：<a href="/wiki/%E8%8C%83%E7%95%B4%E8%AE%BA" title="范畴论">范畴论</a>和<a href="/wiki/%E6%80%81%E5%B0%84" title="态射">态射</a></div>
<p>在<a href="/wiki/%E8%8C%83%E7%95%B4%E8%AE%BA" title="范畴论">范畴论</a>中，函数的槪念被推广为<a href="/wiki/%E6%80%81%E5%B0%84" title="态射">态射</a>的槪念。
</p><p>一个<a href="/wiki/%E7%AF%84%E7%96%87_(%E6%95%B8%E5%AD%B8)" title="范畴 (数学)">范畴</a>包括一组物件与一组态射，每一个态射是个三元组(<i>X</i>, <i>Y</i>, <i>f</i>)，<i>X</i>称为源物件（定义域的类比），<i>Y</i>称为目标物件（到达域的类比），而源物件与目标物件是范畴内的物件。基于这种解释，可以把函数看作<a href="/wiki/%E9%9B%86%E5%90%88%E8%8C%83%E7%95%B4" title="集合范畴">集合范畴</a>里面的态射。
</p>

Husch, <a href="/wiki/%E7%94%B0%E7%B4%8D%E8%A5%BF%E5%A4%A7%E5%AD%B8" title="田纳西大学">田纳西大学</a>（2001年）</li></ul>

<li><a class="external text" href="http://functions.wolfram.com/" rel="nofollow">Wolfram函数网站</a>（<a class="external text" href="//web.archive.org/web/20071010025724/http://functions.wolfram.com/" rel="nofollow">页面存档备份</a>，存于<a href="/wiki/%E4%BA%92%E8%81%94%E7%BD%91%E6%A1%A3%E6%A1%88%E9%A6%86" title="互联网档案馆">互联网档案馆</a>），汇集了各数学函数的公式和图像</li>
